  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_b568f5f1-058f-4d22-80f7-d30472f8f9a2'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer1724723904526297984"><p>The most valuable lesson Emerson Moore ever learned was from her parents: Never get too attached to someone else. That’s why this hard-partying college student plays by her own code of bedroom conduct, refusing to stay with the same guy for too long. She gets all the pleasure of having a good time without the messiness of a relationship.. So what if frat house–hopping has </p></span>
  <span id="freeText1724723904526297984" style="display:none"><p>The most valuable lesson Emerson Moore ever learned was from her parents: Never get too attached to someone else. That’s why this hard-partying college student plays by her own code of bedroom conduct, refusing to stay with the same guy for too long. She gets all the pleasure of having a good time without the messiness of a relationship.. So what if frat house–hopping has earned her a certain reputation around campus? At least no one gets hurt this way—especially her.</p><p>When ridiculously gorgeous Jaxon Riley moves in next door, Emerson’s not sure how long her vow against emotional intimacy can last. Jaxon’s tattoo, muscles, and sexy voice make him tempting, but he also seems to really understand her…until his jealous ex-girlfriend and Emerson’s life-changing discovery about her parents get thrown into the mix. After everything she’s been through, can Emerson handle a real relationship? Or will breaking her rules just lead to a broken heart?</p><p>
  <b>Revised edition: This edition of <i>Beautiful Broken Rules</i> includes editorial revisions.</b>
</p></span>

<div id="review_613297652" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/613297652" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/613297652?book_show_action=true">May 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/17729712-beautiful-broken-rules">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer613297652" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17703716105472641380"><b>5 ‘OMG I LOVED this book’ stars!!! :D </b><br/><br/>Before starting this review- I just want to say this book was AMAZING, FANTASTIC! I just loved it! A HUGE thanks to the author, Kimberly Lauren for providing me with an arc :D <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505953502i/23974764.jpg' width='400' height='530' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Emerson Moore knows who she is...<br/><i>
  <blockquote>One thing I know for sure and have come to terms with- I’m the school <b>slut.</b>
</blockquote>
</i><br/>Em is a junior at college. After tragically losing both of her parents at 15, she has learned not to get close to anyone. You will just get hurt in the end. The only excepti</span>
  <span id="freeText17703716105472641380" style="display:none"><b>5 ‘OMG I LOVED this book’ stars!!! :D </b><br><br>Before starting this review- I just want to say this book was AMAZING, FANTASTIC! I just loved it! A HUGE thanks to the author, Kimberly Lauren for providing me with an arc :D <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505953502i/23974764.jpg" width="400" height="530" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Emerson Moore knows who she is...<br><i>
  <blockquote>One thing I know for sure and have come to terms with- I’m the school <b>slut.</b>
</blockquote>
</i><br>Em is a junior at college. After tragically losing both of her parents at 15, she has learned not to get close to anyone. You will just get hurt in the end. The only exceptions are her step mother Ellie, her step sister Quinn, and her best friend Cole. She does not do relationships. Never has, never will. Em might sleep around, but she has some standards, some rules. She knows exactly where she stands. This protects her and the guy. She never breaks her rules. No matter what.<br><b>
  <blockquote>I have three rules:<br> 1- Never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for<br>2- Never sleep with someone who is in a known relationship.<br>3- Never sleep with someone more than three times.</blockquote>
</b><br>She never wants to. Until she meets him...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505953502i/23974763.jpg" width="400" height="530" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jaxon has moved from Texas with his twin brother Jace on a football scholarship. He and Jace are close friends with Cole and they move into his apartment with him... which happens to be right next door to Em and Quinns. Em and Jaxon hit it off right away. They become fast friends. They are both extremely attracted to one another. After weeks of just hanging out and studying together, the inevitable happens. Jax knows all about Emerson’s rules, he doesn’t like them, but he tries his best not to push her, even though he is developing real feelings for her. He wants to keep her safe, he hates the way people talk to her and treat her. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I don’t need a protector, okay?”<br> “I’m trying my fucking hardest here, Beautiful.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br> I just love Jaxon. Freaking hot as hell, and totally swoonworthy! After a lot of back and forth, Em can’t deny she wants Jax. And more than three times. She can’t be his ‘girlfriend’ or commit to him, but she just wants to be with him and only him. He can accept that... for now. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505953502i/23974762.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Of course there is some drama along the way and some serious angst, but I still loved every second of this book! One of the best NA books I’ve read in a long time. I can’t believe this was a debut novel. Jax and Emerson’s story was sweet, sexy, beautiful and heartbreaking. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505953743i/23974774.jpg" width="400" height="319" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Emerson puts herself out there for the first time. She trust Jax not to break her heart. She knows that he is the only one for her. As much as I loved Jax, he had some frustrating moments, but he came around.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505953743i/23974773.jpg" width="400" height="334" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And what he did to her text book... I think I fell in love with him then!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505953743i/23974772.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One thing I loved about this book is that even though the story has been ‘done before’ its actually pretty original. We’ve all read tons of stories about the self proclaimed manwhore’s (who I LOVE) that change their ways for the right girl, but what about the sluts out there? I loved Emerson. She was a slut, yes, but she owned it. And it only took the right guy to break down her barriers. Once I started this book I just couldn’t put it down! I didn’t want it to end. The two main characters were fantastic, but so were the others. I loved Cole, Jace, and Quinn. Especially Cole, best guy ever! Yep- pretty much loved everything about this one! I highly recommend :D<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505953743i/23974775.jpg" width="400" height="530" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="17703716105472641380" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_646238009" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/646238009" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/646238009?book_show_action=true">Sep 27, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audio CD 9781501230516" href="/book/show/23431329-beautiful-broken-rules">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=kindle-unlimited">kindle-unlimited</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer646238009" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13352205650294346600">I've said it before, and I'll say it again...a narrator can make or break a story. This book is a prime example of a pretty good story that became a mediocre listening experience, solely because the male main characters voice was so bad that I wanted to cover my ears. By all accounts, he should have been a very sexy character. However, I'm pretty sure the narrator for his character made my ovaries shrivel up.<br/><br/>If you can overlook horrible narration or, better yet, you choose to read the story vs. </span>
  <span id="freeText13352205650294346600" style="display:none">I've said it before, and I'll say it again...a narrator can make or break a story. This book is a prime example of a pretty good story that became a mediocre listening experience, solely because the male main characters voice was so bad that I wanted to cover my ears. By all accounts, he should have been a very sexy character. However, I'm pretty sure the narrator for his character made my ovaries shrivel up.<br /><br />If you can overlook horrible narration or, better yet, you choose to read the story vs. listening, it is actually pretty good. In fact, it might have even been pretty great. I definitely would've given this story a 4-star rating if it hadn't been for the fact that I listened to the Audible edition and Jaxon's voice was so off-putting.<br /><br />This is the first YA/NA that I've read in awhile. I find that the youthful, "everything's the end of the world" thinking and immaturity has started to grate on my nerves more than it used to. It's a "not you, it's me" type of thing. My tastes have just changed some.<br /><br />That being said, I do still enjoy a book in this romance sub-genre every once in a while. After all, variety is the spice of life! Sometimes a shallow, "fluffy" read is just what I need to offset the darker reads that I prefer.<br /><br />'Beautiful Broken Rules' was like many other college-aged romances in a lot of ways. Big man on campus smitten with pretty girl, lots of partying, strong supporting characters/friends, back and forth drama.--You know the drill. <br /><br />Yet, there were some pretty big differences in this story that made it stand out from the rest. Most noticeably, the heroine had slept with most of the school's guys. No slut-shaming here, but Emerson was extremely promiscuous. I pitied her. There are very few authors that do a good job of selling a heroine with so little self-respect, but Kimberly Lauren did.<br /><br />Of course, there is a deep, dark emotional reason for Emerson's risky sexual behavior. Before you go there, I'll let you know that it has nothing to do with sexual abuse either. Nope, this girl has chosen sex as her coping tool. She's set some rules to prevent her from ever getting to attached to any one particular person. In essence, she's a slut by design.<br /><br />Jaxon is the new, football star on campus. He has girls fawning over him day and night, but he's only interested in the beautiful girl who walked out of a fraternity house without her shirt on when he first arrived. Yep, "Mr. Perfect" was drawn to her confident demeanor as she did the walk of shame! From that point forward, he decided that he was going to get Emerson to break her stupid rules.<br /><br />Along the way, there was plenty of angst and drama. Jaxon has his own skeletons and his past comes back to haunt him. They spend plenty of time working against each other also. It's like they just can't get in sync with one another. He's hot, she's cold and vice versa.<br /><br />While their on and off behavior was incredibly frustrating at times, it certainly kept things interesting. You've gotta have some push and pull in a story and this one delivered in a big way. <br /><br />I also liked the fact that Jaxon had to actually work a little to get back into Emerson's good graces. In fact, they both had to suffer a little for their mistakes. Fair is fair. If I have to experience the heartache, then I expect my characters to pony up a little pain as well. Nothing makes me madder than having a ton of heartache that is forgotten with a simple apology. It makes me feel like everything I just felt was invalidated. Luckily, that didn't happen with this story. Of course, I would've liked a bit more groveling, but that's just me. <br /><br />I give the story 4-stars. The narration only gets 2-stars from me. This is one that is pretty good, but I wouldn't recommend the audiobook version.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13352205650294346600" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

           <span class="uitext reviewText">People who want to read something cute and are a college romance fan! :D</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer613653236" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6730667287295642064"><b>4.5 Stars~</b><br/><br/><i>I have the biggest stupidest grin on my face; <b>This book was just... *deep breath* ... *sigh* ... AMAZING.</b> I am a major sucker for college romance books and this novel hit spot on!<br/><br/>I mean books like these are the ones which just make the heart melt and make a girl blush and giggle and fall in love.</i><br/><br/><b>Brilliant, Brilliant, Brilliant debut novel..</b> Its so nice to read such a normal book with this whole BDSM era thingie on.. (I mean its nice the bdsm novels, but its get too much at a point of t</span>
  <span id="freeText6730667287295642064" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars~</b><br><br><i>I have the biggest stupidest grin on my face; <b>This book was just... *deep breath* ... *sigh* ... AMAZING.</b> I am a major sucker for college romance books and this novel hit spot on!<br><br>I mean books like these are the ones which just make the heart melt and make a girl blush and giggle and fall in love.</i><br><br><b>Brilliant, Brilliant, Brilliant debut novel..</b> Its so nice to read such a normal book with this whole BDSM era thingie on.. (I mean its nice the bdsm novels, but its get too much at a point of time)<br><br>I miss watching a good chick-flick or a nice romantic movie; people seriously make shit now a days.. but THANK GOD for such books.. They totally feed my addiction.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421322ra/836788.gif" width="240" height="180" alt="intresting" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was such a wonderful book, so beautifully written with such amazing characters. The story line, the plot and each and every drama filled twist and turn was brilliant. It wasn't like any twists and turns were purposely added, it all flowed so smoothly and formed such an amazing story!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Be silly, be honest, and be kind,”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>This book was about these 5 amazing friends;Emerson, Quinn, Jaxon, Cole and Jace &amp; their journey in life.<br>I swear each and every character, even the side non-existent ones were amazing!! :D<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Em-<br>I have Three Rules:<br>•Never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for,<br>•Never sleep with someone who is in a known relationship and finally,<br>•Never sleep with someone more than three times.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>She broke only 1 rule and there starts her story~<br><br>I really liked Emerson, she wasn't a blonde damsel in distress type! She was a bold girl, A slut as she believe she was. She enjoyed sex, so no harm no foul when she isn't doing it the wrong way ;)<br>I really liked her character. She was not the whiney immature idiots we come across. She was NICE!<br><br>Jaxon, HELL BOY!! I wanted to gobble him up for breakfast lunch dinner and dessert. He was just AMAZING, charming, awesome and OH SO SWEET! ;))<br><br>Quinn and Cole and Jace; The type of best friends you'd give a limb to have!<br><br>I loved each and every relationship this book had, this book was so peaceful and calming..<br>I seriously didn't want this book to end, like when we reached the HEA part I was like NOOOOOOO have a continuity or something, PLEASE; because the story was soo good I wanted it to just go on and on! ;D<br>I reallllly hope it continues, like with Jace maybe so we can read more about this gang because they were BEAUTIFUL. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I want you.”<br>“Only me?”<br>“Only you.”<br>~<br>“You’re my heart. You don’t walk away from your heart,”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Gah, I swear Emerson and Jaxon were so cute, I was only blushing and giggling throughout. :D<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421322ra/836789.gif" width="360" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>I can’t wait to jump back into this world and I hope you come back. - KL</i><br>I'll be looking forward to more stuff by this Author. :D <br>I mean, I rarely do we get to read such an amazing debut novel by a self-published author.<br>~<br><br><br>Thank you Kimberly Lauren for providing me with the ARC to review your wonderful novel.</span>

<div id="review_615671269" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/615671269" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/615671269?book_show_action=true">May 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/17729712-beautiful-broken-rules">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=book-1-of-my-fav-series">book-1-of-my-fav-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer615671269" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8606618771960165053"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421620i/837754._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>First, here's my casting:<br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421620i/837755._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421620i/837756._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ** 4.5 stars!<br/><br/><strong>SQUEEE!!! Bad boy fans, you're going to love this book!! <br/><br/><em>Beautiful Broken Rules </em>was a wonderfully addictive and romantic read with a bad boy hero who I promise you will fall for! There was heaps of swoon, awesome banter, and a delicious kind of angst that made my heart race and kept me flipping pages. Once I started, I could <em>not</em> put it down! </strong><br/><br/>I had been in such a reading funk the last few days. I'd started and stopped so many books t</span>
  <span id="freeText8606618771960165053" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421620i/837754._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First, here's my casting:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421620i/837755._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421620i/837756._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ** 4.5 stars!<br><br><strong>SQUEEE!!! Bad boy fans, you're going to love this book!! <br><br><em>Beautiful Broken Rules </em>was a wonderfully addictive and romantic read with a bad boy hero who I promise you will fall for! There was heaps of swoon, awesome banter, and a delicious kind of angst that made my heart race and kept me flipping pages. Once I started, I could <em>not</em> put it down! </strong><br><br>I had been in such a reading funk the last few days. I'd started and stopped so many books that I was starting to wonder if it was 'me', y'know? But THIS BOOK pulled me right back into happy reader land!<br><br>Fans of <em>Beautiful Disaster</em> should definitely check this book out! Although the plot lines are very different, this one gave me many of those same wonderful 'feelings'.<br><br>This book also pretty much defied one of the norms because instead of having a manwhore hero, we had a heroine who pretty much was the female equivalent. Kinda weird to think of it when the roles are reversed, huh? But it totally worked for this character. Emerson was a strong heroine and I loved that she didn't make any excuses for the way she was and the things she did.<br><br>Ok, I'm getting ahead of myself here...<br><br>The book is about Emerson, a college student who has three rules that she never breaks: 1) Never sleep with someone a friend has feelings for, 2) Never sleep with someone in a known relationship, 3) Never sleep with the same person more than three times. These rules keep her 'safe' within her comfort zone. She was deeply scarred by events in her past that basically left her terrified of relationships and so these rules are her coping mechanism that both allow her to have fun and keep her clear of being bogged down in any relationship drama or heart break.<br><br>Until Jaxon Riley showed up.<br><br>With his gorgeous tattoos, his cocky but endearing attitude, and his naturally protectiveness, this bad boy sweetheart spun her world right around and for the first time in her life, she found herself actually <em>wanting</em> more than just a fling. He didn't care about her past, he just wanted her future and was determined to win her heart.<br><br>*swoons*<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I don't need a protector, okay?" I breathed.</em>
    <br>
    <em>"I'm trying my fucking hardest here, Beautiful."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Only a few pages into this book and I knew it was going to be a winner! I was smiling and chuckling and swooning and it just kept on getting better. I really honestly loved pretty much everything about it.<br><br>I fell hard for Jax. Everything about him was either alluring, intriguing, or downright hot! And Emerson was a surprising and fun heroine. She certainly had her share of issues but I felt like I could understand them and better yet, <em>Jax</em> understood them and I seriously just loved the way he was with. So sweet and tender but yet totally possessive and protective. The perfect combination! He knew about her issues and yet he was willing to be patient with her.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>“I love you... Relax, I won’t say it again for a while. I just want you to get used to the fact that one day, when you’re comfortable with it, I’ll tell you every day, multiple times a day. I want you to know how much I love you every single damn day, but for now, I’ll just let you soak it in.” </em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I loved that this was more than just a romance. The core group of friends and family were just as awesome to read about. Some of their scenes were seriously just priceless!<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"Ew, guys, stop it. Not on the couch." Quinn was right next to us, batting me off of Jaxon.</em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>"Oh, like we haven't gotten plenty of fluids on this couch already, sweetheart," Cole laughed from behind her.</em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>"All of you are disgusting, shut up, push play and keep your fluids to yourselves," Jace complained.</em>
</blockquote><br>There were definite undercurrents of tension though through the story because of how Emerson clearly shied away from all relationships and there were some moments of full on angst and drama but at the same time, all of it was the delicious kind. I revelled in it even though there were times when I just wanted to shove her and Jax into a room together and not let them out until they'd worked through their issues.<br><br>One thing that I did really like was that throughout the drama, I never once doubted their feelings for each other and despite being a tad frustrated at how long it took them to get through their last issue, because I could tell they were still just crazy about each other, it allowed me to ride it all out with a good feeling instead of being worried sick. They both made mistakes but I also *knew* they'd work things out and was excited to see it all come together.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <strong>
      <em>"You're my heart. You don't walk away from your heart."</em>
    </strong>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><em>Beautiful Broken Rules</em> was exactly what I'd been looking for. A fun, delicious blend of swoon and angst with a possessive but sweet bad boy and a strong but damaged heroine. It just pushed all the right buttons for me and is definitely one of my new favorite New Adult romance reads.<br><br>Highly recommended!<br><br>4.5 stars<br><br>PS - This reads as a standalone but there will be more spin-off books about the side characters. The first will be about Jax's brother Jace. I can't wait!!<br><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4685996349723599189">SPOILER FREE REVIEW -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br/>4 STARS out of 5<br/>Genre: New Adult Romance/College<br/><br/>LOVED IT! New Adult at its finest!<br/><br/><i>
  <b>‘One thing I know for sure and have come to terms with– I’m the school slut. I hate that word; but sometimes it is what it is, or in my situation, I am what I am. I like guys, all kinds of them and lots of them. College has been the perfect setting for being able to meet so many. Since I have no desire for a relationship whatsoever, I sleep around.</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText4685996349723599189" style="display:none">SPOILER FREE REVIEW -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br>4 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: New Adult Romance/College<br><br>LOVED IT! New Adult at its finest!<br><br><i>
  <b>‘One thing I know for sure and have come to terms with– I’m the school slut. I hate that word; but sometimes it is what it is, or in my situation, I am what I am. I like guys, all kinds of them and lots of them. College has been the perfect setting for being able to meet so many. Since I have no desire for a relationship whatsoever, I sleep around. Sleeping with one guy consistently is too permanent.’<br></b>
</i> ~Em<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417042i/824380.jpg" alt=" photo ce29281b-9cff-4d3b-9b0c-b97b5bab7ba6_zps113e3968.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417042i/824381.jpg" alt=" photo eb591923-8171-4dec-9e7d-a0d5b53e84cd_zps5defca34.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>HOLD UP. <br><br>PAUSE. <br><br>All I kept hearing when I started reading this was Promiscuous girl By Nelly Furtado<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417042ra/824382.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m7sustju9h1r1c49to1_500_zpsb48cfe49.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417042ra/824383.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lqws2bvtZj1qjmg4no1_500_zpse9da839f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417042ra/824384.gif" alt=" photo 1199864_o_zps78d5f875.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>LOL! I cannot be the only one who heard that song while reading. <br>Am I?*shrugs*<br><br><b>Ok back to my review</b><br><br>Beautiful Broken Rules is a fun sexy New Adult read with a nice spin on role reversal. Emerson Moore is the school slut (her words not mines) She does not do boyfriends and she has pretty much sworn off love. Sound familiar? Because I swear the guys I read about in books all seem to live by the words<br> <br><b>“I don’t do love”<br><br>“I will never fall in love”<br><br>“Why buy the cow when you can get the milk for FREE”</b><br><br>Oh and let’s not forget this one<br><br><b>“I never hit the same honey pot twice” </b><br><br>The male characters I love live by these words as if each phrase is the male national anthem or some shit. <b> WHAT. EVER.</b><br>My girl Emerson has her own rules to live by to make life easier… <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417042i/824385.jpg" alt=" photo 8debd287-4b7a-448d-9278-2364ec98c11f_zps4406c55c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That’s right, she likes to play boys but you can only have her for a limited amount of time. 3 rounds and your OUT, this way nobody's feelings get hurt once playtime ends.<br><br>And everything is going well until she meets Jaxon. A guy rumored to be the male version of her. Jaxon oozes sex appeal without even opening his mouth. That cocky grin alone will have your panties in a twist. Jaxon just moved to Cali from Texas and is attending the same school as Emerson on a football scholarship. He’ll also be her new neighbor! Can you say HELL YES!<br><br>Jaxon meets all of my bad boy criteria’s<br><br><b>-He’s a TOTAL ALPHA<br>-He's intelligent <br>-He rides a motorcycle <br>–He has a voice that can drop panties <br>–He has a body built for sin <br>–He has a tattoo <br>–He plays football(athlete) </b><br><br>*Screams* TOTAL PACKAGE! I mean really what more can a girl ask for! *le sigh*<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417042i/824386.jpg" alt=" photo 4ddfc7d1-cc1a-4375-8ab6-33748ec0d669_zps704d49de.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Emerson and Jaxon dance a nice slow tango with flirty twist, cocky turns and witty banter filled dips, where each of them takes the turn at lead. Jax knows her rules and he is willing to dance along. That is until he realizes he wants more. Unfortunately Emerson fights being more than friends tooth and nail. Her past showed her that love is nothing but pain, secrets and heartache. <br><br>She has been able to do her thing so why risk the chance of hurting someone, or being the one who ends up hurt. Logical thinking right? To bad the heart wants what the heart wants.<br><br>When her best friend Quinn notices a change in Emerson because of Jax; she tells her to give a relationship a chance.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Just the fact that you care enough not to hurt him shows me that maybe you can handle one.”</i>
</b> -Quinn<br><br>Em nixes that idea with the quickness. <br><br><i>
  <b>“I don’t want to handle one…”</b>
</i> -Em<br><br>Jax does not give up though and Em starts to catch feelings but just like she knew it would secrets, pain and heartache follow.<br><br><b>The chemistry between Jaxon and Emerson is H O T!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417042ra/824387.gif" alt=" photo fansself_zps7249e965.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>The sex between Jaxon and Emerson… HOT! </b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>‘We were grabbing at each other like we needed to be inside of one another, as if we needed the other one to breathe.’</i>
</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417042i/824388.jpg" alt=" photo c72503d5-fe1b-4fc3-8507-3f05d62cd360_zps14916c59.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>“Tell me that you want me,”</b>
</i> he whispered. <br><i>
  <b>“I want you.”</b>
</i> Always. <br><i>
  <b>“Only me?”</b>
</i><br><b>
  <i> “Only you.”</i>
</b> Had there ever been anyone else?<br><br><br>All steam aside I really enjoyed this New Adult read, essentially all Kimberly Lauren did was take the man whore concept we all love and flip it.<u> And guess what?</u><b> IT WORKS!</b> She gives us great secondary characters that pull you in even more, a<i> sweet</i> secondary love story and the promise for a book 2 most likely featuring Jace, which I will happily read!<br><br><br><u>My thoughts</u><br>Overall this was a fun read and I look forward to more work by Kimberly Lauren! I recommend this to all of my friends who enjoy a good NA read!<br><br><br>My Ratings<br>Characters- Lovable sexy and witty<br>Writing Style- Good, I just can't get enough<br>Plot/Storyline- Role reversal, GENIUS<br>Steam Factor- Hot/Very Steamy<br>Overall- I loved it!! If you haven't yet, READ IT!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br>For more reviews got to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a><br><b>*Copy kindly provided by author in exchange for an honest review*</b></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer617053191" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16320363386517683238">5 Beautiful Stars!!!!<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421825i/838502.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>If you are a fan of angsty and steamy NA, drop everything you're doing and read this book! Seriously! I am still flabbergasted that this is a debut novel. I kept going back to the author's page several times to make sure I didn't miss something. WOW!<br/><br/>Emerson Moore is the school slut. But she does have a few standards when it comes to hooking up.<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for, never sleep with someone who is in a known relationship, and finally</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText16320363386517683238" style="display:none">5 Beautiful Stars!!!!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421825i/838502.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you are a fan of angsty and steamy NA, drop everything you're doing and read this book! Seriously! I am still flabbergasted that this is a debut novel. I kept going back to the author's page several times to make sure I didn't miss something. WOW!<br><br>Emerson Moore is the school slut. But she does have a few standards when it comes to hooking up.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for, never sleep with someone who is in a known relationship, and finally, never sleep with someone more than three times.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I was intrigued with this character. She didn't hide who she was, or feel ashamed of it. She was also incredibly endearing. Emerson was just the right amount of tough shell hiding a vulnerable center. She sleeps around, and owns it. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I've accepted who I am. The girl who will never become serious about anyone, who will enjoy life, have fun with guys along the way and never get her heart broken</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>She doesn't want to open herself up to get hurt, because she knows that eventually all relationships end.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>There's no point in having a relationship, because if they aren't cheating, they're dying.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>When Emerson meets Jaxon Riley, she finds herself questioning her rules.<br><br>I really enjoyed the reversal of roles in this book. We have a female that is a player and hiding demons of her past behind her tough-girl persona. Jaxon pursues her in a very understated but effective way. This was not a case of insta-love. I found their relationship to be very believable for a college romance.<br><br>Ever since they first meet, they feel an instant pull, an attraction towards each other. Unable to resist, they give into the lust and It.Was.Steamy<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421825ra/838503.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But Jaxon is not satisfied with having just a small part of Emerson, and he is determined to break through her walls.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Damn it, Emerson, just stop!" he yelled. "Stop pretending you don't care. Why won't you let me in? Why won't you let me care about you? Because for some maddening reason, I do!"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Little by little, he begins to tear her down. Through some very swoon-worthy moments and gestures, Jaxon begins to show Emerson that maybe love just might be worth the chance.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421825i/838504.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With each kiss, each note, each whisper, Jaxon crumbles more and more of Emerson's defensive walls.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Emerson, tell me what you want."<br>"I don't know how."<br>"Tell me that you want me," he whispered.<br>"I want you." Always.<br>"Only me?"<br>"Only you." Had there ever been anyone else?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421825ra/838505.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jaxon and Emerson's relationship was by no means perfect. There were moments throughout this book that I wanted to strangle either one or both of them. There was so much angst and pain that could have been avoided had they only communicated better. But then this book wouldn't have been what it was.<br><br>The love between them isn't perfect, but it was an amazing journey to read.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Before I'd gotten to know you, I knew I had to make you mine. It only got worse the closer we got. I realized you weren't mine at all. I. AM. YOURS."<br>He grabbed each side of my face and looked into my eyes. "you don't walk away from your heart."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421825i/838506.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really loved all the supporting characters as well and I sincerely hope that the author would make this into a series. I'd love to get Jace's book. Oh, did I not mention that Jaxon has an identical twin brother, Jace? Yup! There's 2 of them!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16320363386517683238" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10841393417731429911"><br/><br/>Emerson Moore is the school slut. She knows it and accepts it, because its the truth...<br/>She likes it that way, have a good time, no expectations and a guaranteed good time.<br/><br/>Emerson:<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421511i/837367._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>She has Rules:<br/><br/><b>"I have three rules: never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for, never sleep with someone who is in a known relationship (when this isn't disclosed to me, it is not my fault), and finally, never sleep with someone more than three times."</b><br/><br/>The rules have been set to avoid demons from her past..<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421511i/837368.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>He</span>
  <span id="freeText10841393417731429911" style="display:none"><br><br>Emerson Moore is the school slut. She knows it and accepts it, because its the truth...<br>She likes it that way, have a good time, no expectations and a guaranteed good time.<br><br>Emerson:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421511i/837367._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She has Rules:<br><br><b>"I have three rules: never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for, never sleep with someone who is in a known relationship (when this isn't disclosed to me, it is not my fault), and finally, never sleep with someone more than three times."</b><br><br>The rules have been set to avoid demons from her past..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421511i/837368.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Her parents were married and divorced when she was 15yrs old and they both died in the same car accident.<br>Em assumes they were having an affair when they died. She would never hurt herself or anyone ever. So she sticks to her rules.<br>The only person who she let's in is her step sister Quinn.<br><br>That's until her best friend Cole's two friends move into the apartment next door to her. They twins..<br>Jaxon and Jace Riley...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421511i/837369.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After being friends with Jax, the sexual chemistry is electric. Not only is Jax smoking hot, they get on well and are such good friends, but for Em its not enough...<br>So Em does what she does best- she fcuks him.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421511i/837370.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then she tells him the rules...<br><br>He doesn't like it but he accepts it.<br>Jax doesn't want to push Em away..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421511i/837371._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>When Jax starts flirting with other girls Em gets jealous, she hates herself for getting jealous because it goes against her rules- never get attached.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421511i/837372.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jax wants Em to let him in but she Runs!<br><i>YEP Another Runner! Lmao! </i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421511i/837373.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She runs from her feelings for Jax because she can't be his girlfriend! She doesn't do relationships.<br><br>But she's only fooling herself- because she wants Jax and him only...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421511ra/837374.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Tell me that you want me,” he whispered."<br>"I want you.” Always.<br>"Only me?”<br><br>"Only you.” Had there ever been anyone else?</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421511i/837375.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She makes stupid mistakes along the way and after putting herself out there for the first time, she gets her heart broken.<br>These two definitely need to communicate more about their past or they wouldn't have been in the situations they were in. <br><br><b>
  <i>"It’s what you do with it once you’ve screwed up that matters."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421511i/837376.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I admit Jax made me so angry at times but like Em, he was also scared.<br><br><b>“It's impossible. I can't be your friend. It hurts too much. If I'm ruining you, then you've destroyed me. I finally trusted someone enough to love and you proved that all along it wasn't worth it."</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[After pain, tears and heartbreak- Jaxx and Em break down their barriers and the walls around their hearts and let each other in. <br><br><b>“You're my heart. You don't walk away from your heart," he whispered in my ear.” </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421511i/837377._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This book is totally addicting and so well written, I am shocked this is a debut novel- the writing, the banter between Emerson and her friends is really funny at times.<br>This book has really strong sweet characters who you can't help but love to: Jace, Cole, Quinn. Hell in the end I even liked Micah! :)<br><br>If you looking for a Great NA book, this is it!<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer616202217" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16613017970003015048">4 BREAKING THE RULES STARS.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421701i/838094._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>A likeable slut? Who would have thought. <br/><br/>Readers let me introduce you to Emerson 'Em' Moore ~ pretty, intelligent, popular and yes the ermm college slut. She battles with the concept of a long term arrangement after being scarred by her parents unfortunate separation, nasty divorce and eventual heartache. Nobody will break down those walls she's built around her heart. See she's got it all figured out, she's got rules. Things were in place, people knew where she stood,</span>
  <span id="freeText16613017970003015048" style="display:none">4 BREAKING THE RULES STARS.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421701i/838094._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A likeable slut? Who would have thought. <br><br>Readers let me introduce you to Emerson 'Em' Moore ~ pretty, intelligent, popular and yes the ermm college slut. She battles with the concept of a long term arrangement after being scarred by her parents unfortunate separation, nasty divorce and eventual heartache. Nobody will break down those walls she's built around her heart. See she's got it all figured out, she's got rules. Things were in place, people knew where she stood, order and routine had its place that was until she met ...<br><br>Jaxon Riley, tattooed, blue eyed college frat boy and football star. From first meeting with Emerson it was 'want' at first sight. This college boy was not giving up anytime soon and he certainly won't play by the rules ...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421701i/838095._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421701i/838096._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Knee deep in sweet is my thing so this short, stateside novel ticked my romance boxes. The characters were interesting, the relationships were adorable and Chemistry certainly played its part.<br><br>This book for me was the perfect 'filler'. A book that was easy and uncomplicated . If you need predictable, sweet and another book boyfriend to add to your list, then Jump right in to this college romance. 'beautiful broken rules' was cute sexy and funny with just enough angst served on the side to make an interesting plot.<br><br>❤❤ "be silly, be honest, and be kind."<br><br>4 stars and a book heart filled to the brim.</span>

<div id="review_614778383" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/614778383" />
    <a title="Anna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6744426-anna"><img alt="Anna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442117297p2/6744426.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/614778383?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna" href="/user/show/6744426-anna">Anna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/17729712-beautiful-broken-rules">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">anyone looking for college-aged angst</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6744426-anna?shelf=christy-jacked-me-upppp">christy-jacked-me-upppp</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer614778383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer209391052840221748">~ 5 gorgeous **BLUE EYES BRING HAPPINESS AS DEEP AS THE SEAS** ~<br/><br/><b>JAXON</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421489i/837317.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421489i/837318.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421489i/837319.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I LOVED this book! it had me girl-fanning and all kinds of WORKED UP !<br/><br/>Emerson<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421489i/837320.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>The girl I loved to HATE <br/><br/>NOT the usual female lead. <div id="review_610917555" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/610917555" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/610917555?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/17729712-beautiful-broken-rules">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer610917555" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10146489517923484705"><b>
  <i>”I really hope I don’t screw this up..”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420923i/835624._SY540_.jpg' width='320' height='310' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Emerson Moore follows three simple rules to protect herself from attachments and heart break: <br/><br/><b>Rule 1~“Never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for”<br/>Rule 2~ “Never sleep with someone who is in a known relationship.”<br/>Rule 3 ~ “Never sleep with someone more than three times.”</b><br/><br/>You see, her parents’ death left her so broken that she protects/guards herself from getting too attached to guys and vice versa. Unlike a lot of main characters that I have r</span>
  <span id="freeText10146489517923484705" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>”I really hope I don’t screw this up..”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420923i/835624._SY540_.jpg" width="320" height="310" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Emerson Moore follows three simple rules to protect herself from attachments and heart break: <br><br><b>Rule 1~“Never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for”<br>Rule 2~ “Never sleep with someone who is in a known relationship.”<br>Rule 3 ~ “Never sleep with someone more than three times.”</b><br><br>You see, her parents’ death left her so broken that she protects/guards herself from getting too attached to guys and vice versa. Unlike a lot of main characters that I have read to date, Em isn’t shy, quiet or untouchable. She embraces her sexuality and owns it. One side of the coin on being a “slut” is guys discussing her with each other and rumors, reputation…these things don’t phases her. (I had a hard time wrapping my brain around that reaction.) <br><br>Em attends college with her stepsister Quinn their newly acquired best friend Cole. These three are really tight and the book takes off when Cole’s twin best friends from home, Jace and Jaxon move in with Cole and attend the university as well.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420923i/835625._SX540_.jpg" width="380" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kimberly Lauren can sure write sexy jocks!! I absolutely LOVED the sexy banter between Em and Jaxon, which starts from their first encounter. <br><br>Em and Jaxon’s chemistry is supported by a friendship which leads to LOVE…<br><br>Emerson Moore has her first boyfriend y’all! <br><br><b>
  <i>”You have to stop worrying that you’ll lose me. There’s nowhere else in this world that I want to be. I love you, beautiful girl.”</i>
</b><br><br>As you can guess, things don’t go smoothly for Emerson and Jaxon. Jaxon is ALPHA and Em is learning how to face and discuss her feelings. The couple does fall apart…but this story isn’t a cliffhanger and has a nice big HEA.<br><br><b>
  <i>”When Cole carried you away from me that day, I realized you weren’t mine at all. I. AM. YOURS.”</i>
</b><br><br>Overall, Ms. Lauren’s debut novel was sexy and fun. I loved these four friends Cole, Quinn, Jace, Jaxon and Em and I'm totally on board for any future books by this author. <br><br><i>*ARC courtesy of author in exchange for an honest review*</i></span>

She also has three rules for dating guys and she NEVER breaks them.<br/><br/><br/><b>Rule #1 --- > Never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for.<br/><br/><br/>Rule #2 ---- > Never sleep with someo</b></span>
  <span id="freeText1403045333262908094" style="display:none"><br><a href="http://imgur.com/DxW0pRP" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421542i/837485._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>5 Rule Breaking- I Have a HUGE smile on my face- Beautiful Stars</b><br><br><br>There’s a reason why Beautiful Broken Rules has rave reviews and ratings, it’s <b>JUST.THAT.GOOD.</b> If you want a fun, happy, light-hearted read that will truly put you in a good mood, then Beautiful Broken Rules is for you.<br><br><br>Emerson (Emmy) is a slut and knows it. She also has three rules for dating guys and she NEVER breaks them.<br><br><br><b>Rule #1 --- &gt; Never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for.<br><br><br>Rule #2 ---- &gt; Never sleep with someone who is in a known relationship (when this isn’t disclosed to me, it is not my fault)<br><br><br>Rule #3 ---- &gt; Never sleep with someone more than three times.</b><br><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/w11cgpl" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421543i/837486._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Jaxon and his brother Jace are best friends with Emmy’s best friend Cole. This year, Jaxon and Jace move in with Cole, who happens to lives next door to Emmy. Jaxon may be the one to help Emmy reform, if only he can get her to stop pushing him away.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Whatever, your heart knows what I am talking about, and one day your brain will catch up</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>This book was recommended to me by my BBF and she knows I am a very picky person when I read. So when I started the first page, I’ll tell ya…. I WAS HOOKED! From start to finish, there was not a dull moment and this read is completely a page turner.<br><br><br>The number one reason why I loved this book so much is because there is no love triangle and there is no cheating, in fact the main Heroine is very adamant in not cheating. Do I typically like books where the Heroine is a slut? No, but do I like Emmy? YES, in fact I LOVED her and you get why she is the way she is. I love how she is confident, sassy and just doesn’t let people bring her down.<br><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/lSaBhKj" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421543i/837487._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>You reckless, frustratingly beautiful girl, why are you out here all alone?<br><br><br>You deserve to know how great it can be for someone to care about you. I don’t even know what a good relationship is.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>The beginning starts off with Emmy waking up from a hook-up, I know… I shake my head too, but it’s really funny, especially when she can’t find her clothes and yes has a meet cute with Jaxon! Oh Lord, let me tell you about Jaxon, he is so freakin’ swoon-worthy, drool-worthy, I- want-to-ride-his-bike please alpha male (and I have no desire to ride bikes).<br><br><br>Jaxon and Emmy’s “relationship” is adorable. It’s basically Jaxon trying to tame the wild Emmy. And let me tell you …there are no frustrating parts. Emmy doesn’t go in circles and I never wanted to rip my hair out. The writing was smooth, but there was plenty of tension to be engaging and entertaining. I really needed this read after a few dramatic ones. Oh and the side characters, <b>I LOVE THEM</b>. Quinn (Emmy’s best friend), Jace, and Cole, are all awesome and I am stoked about book 2, Jace’s Story.<br><br> <br>Kimberly Lauren is a fantastic writer and if you were on the fence with Beautiful Broken Rules, I am here to take you off your fence. Yes, all five feet and two inches of me will pick you up and take you off. Read it!<br><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/v9xTCRz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421543i/837488.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>For more review and author interview - &gt; <a href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Jacqueline’s Reads</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1403045333262908094" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8569939693408578301"><b> ****** Beautiful Broken Rules is now LIVE!!! <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/Beautiful-Broken-Rules-ebook/dp/B00CS5LLEE/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&qid=1368577745&sr=8-1&keywords=beautiful+broken+rules'>http://www.amazon.com/Beautiful-Broke...</a> </b> <br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><b> So, emotional, heart wrenching, taking you on a roller coaster stars. </b> <br/><br/>Em is the school slut. She knows it and has no problem sleeping around. But there are rules. Certain rules that she goes by so, she will never have to be put in a situation where, she will get attached or hurt. <br/><br/><b> The rules </b> <br/><br/>#1. Never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for. <br/>#2. Never sleep with someone who is in a known relations</span>
  <span id="freeText8569939693408578301" style="display:none"><b> ****** Beautiful Broken Rules is now LIVE!!! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Beautiful-Broken-Rules-ebook/dp/B00CS5LLEE/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1368577745&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=beautiful+broken+rules">http://www.amazon.com/Beautiful-Broke...</a> </b> <br><br><br><br><br><b> So, emotional, heart wrenching, taking you on a roller coaster stars. </b> <br><br>Em is the school slut. She knows it and has no problem sleeping around. But there are rules. Certain rules that she goes by so, she will never have to be put in a situation where, she will get attached or hurt. <br><br><b> The rules </b> <br><br>#1. Never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for. <br>#2. Never sleep with someone who is in a known relationship. <br>#3. Never sleep with someone more than three times. <br><br><b> Meet Em </b><br><br><a href="http://s1321.photobucket.com/user/ambersreadingroom/media/688B8726-5157-42EC-AD4C-2F3BA8DAE302-1268-000000FD948C7A56_zps80fc8829.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Em, is very hard on her rules, never breaks them even if the guy is great in bed. She blocks up this wall around everyone so she won't get hurt, never shows her true feelings because of her past, the demons that have made her this girl.<br><br>Cole is Em's best friend, he lives in the same apartment complex then her and Quinn and now his two best friends from his home town are moving in with him, they all go to college together. Em meets Jax and he is drop dead makes your knees weak sexy. <br><br><b> Meet Jax </b> <br><br><a href="http://s1321.photobucket.com/user/ambersreadingroom/media/DA593BD6-4715-45E6-BE50-3C0422BE404F-1268-000000FD8F106967_zps244b7eeb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I feel in love with Jax the moment Em laid eyes on him. Em has meet her match when it comes to sweet talking Jax. He is a ladies man where the girls just fall to their knees with his sexy voice. <br><br>Breaking down walls to try to be with Em, Jax throws his heart out there so many times, you just watch to bitch slap Em for not seeing it and being so damn scared. <br><br>These two almost gave me a damn heart attack worrying so much about what the other one is going to do. <br><br><b> “He finished quickly, closed my fingers into my palm and kissed them. I slowly uncurled them to read his message, which was written boldly across the expanse of my palm. One word that screamed a whole lot more. <br><br>MINE.” </b> <br><br><a href="http://s1321.photobucket.com/user/ambersreadingroom/media/imagesCA4ZSDCY_zps0fe78947.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>It has been awhile since I read a book that kept me up at night. I stayed up till around 4 in the morning just to finish this book, I did not care if I had to work in a couple of hours. I just know I had to finish this. I was pulled into this within the first couple of pages. It drew me and kept me wound up in such a emotional wreck I was losing it at times.<br><br><a href="http://s1321.photobucket.com/user/ambersreadingroom/media/For%20reviews/tumblr_luxvzsshla1qd94umo1_500_zps75fdd2bd.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I feel such a emotional devotion with these two. It will leave you a wreck at times. I wanted it to happen so damn bad I had tears in my eyes for them... <br><br>Once again they have become part of my favorite little group of characters that I want to lock up and read for my own enjoyment.<br><br>Overall this book is simply amazing... I love it so much. <br><br><i> I received a ARC kindly provided by the Author for exchange for an honest review. </i></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/17729712-beautiful-broken-rules">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer588992604" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4890653762382215109"><i>
  <b>LOVED IT!!</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>Jaxon...</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417437i/825624.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Sexy fine man.. play's football..always been a skirt chaser..love'em and leave'em..<br/><br/><i>Emerson...</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417437i/825625._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>She's the female version of Jaxon....she doesn't mind being the girl that gives it up the most on campus. She enjoys sex and she has nothing to be ashamed about. She's gorgeous and knows it. She's also emotionally unavailable to any man for more than anything but sex. And one of her main rules is to never have sex with one guy more than 3 times... <br/><br/>When Jaxon moves in with his twin a</span>
  <span id="freeText4890653762382215109" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>LOVED IT!!</b>
</i><br><br><i>Jaxon...</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417437i/825624.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Sexy fine man.. play's football..always been a skirt chaser..love'em and leave'em..<br><br><i>Emerson...</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417437i/825625._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>She's the female version of Jaxon....she doesn't mind being the girl that gives it up the most on campus. She enjoys sex and she has nothing to be ashamed about. She's gorgeous and knows it. She's also emotionally unavailable to any man for more than anything but sex. And one of her main rules is to never have sex with one guy more than 3 times... <br><br>When Jaxon moves in with his twin and her best guy friend right next door to her and her sister's apartment, Em knows she'll be sleeping with Jaxon no matter what eventually. The sparks fly the minute they lay eyes on each other. But Jaxon see's more in Emerson than she wants anyone to see... eventually he's breaking down the walls she's built around her heart. He's never wanted one woman before..but now that he's become close to Emerson and..no one else will do. She's it for him...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380809461i/3124314._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Emerson truly struggles to let Jaxon into her heart...but she finally does and she's happier than she's ever been. But as always, her happiness is threatened...she's always looking over her shoulder.. not trusting her feelings or Jaxon's feelings. She's knows she's going to do something to mess it up.<br><br><i>
  <b>“Damn it, Emerson, just stop!” he yelled, “Stop pretending you don’t care. Why won’t you let me in? Why won’t you let me care about you? Because for some maddening reason, I do!”</b>
</i><br><br> She manages to piss Jaxon off enough that he wonders if its all really worth it. The he gives up , after promising Em he never would....and Em is left heartbroken just like she always knew she would be.....<br><br><i>
  <b>“Jaxon, stop saying all of this, it’s not necessary.” I grabbed his waistband again. “I’m going to be better now, I swear. Let me apologize.” I took a deep breath and said, “I love you.” I watched as he winced in pain at my words. That was definitely not the reaction I was hoping for. Just then the gravity of the situation started to hit, so I lowered my voice to a whisper as I looked up at him. “Don’t do this, I love you.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417437ra/825626.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Now don't freak out.. this is an HEA so of course they don't stay apart for long... they both still love each other and live next door to each other so neither can get very far. Jaxon soon realizes the mistake he made letting her walk away and Em realizes she never should have walked to begin with.. <br><br>You know what you are getting when you read this story....falling in love, messing it up, then putting it all together again. This one had some angst but nothing it really wasn't to bad at all. I really loved Emerson and Jaxon's journey together and the sweet HEA made me smile and sigh out loud.. This was a good one.. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380809461i/3124315.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b>“Tell me that you want me,” he whispered. “I want you.” Always. “Only me?” “Only you.” Had there ever been anyone else?</b>
</i><br><br><i>
  <b>I grabbed both of his hands and interlocked my fingers with his.   “You said you thought you made me weaker and that’s just not true. You make me stronger. You make me appreciate what I have and want to be a better person for you.”</b>
</i><br><br><i>The End...</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="4890653762382215109" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
