<div id="review_615689594" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/615689594" />
    <a title="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3716081-it-s-just-me-shelly-b"><img alt="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374929701p2/3716081.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/615689594?book_show_action=true">May 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" href="/user/show/3716081-it-s-just-me-shelly-b">It&#39;s just me Shelly B</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/17729712-beautiful-broken-rules">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer615689594" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13555356797914753694"><br/><i>Emerson</i>......<br/><br/><b>“I have three rules: never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for, never sleep with someone who is in a known relationship (when this isn't disclosed to me, it is not my fault), and finally, never sleep with someone more than three times."</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421623i/837769.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>She's the school slut but she's ok with that because she hates or just refuses to be in a relationship. So she made some rules and she tries to stick by them. She's lost important people in her life and she doesn't want to go through tha</span>
  <span id="freeText13555356797914753694" style="display:none"><br><i>Emerson</i>......<br><br><b>“I have three rules: never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for, never sleep with someone who is in a known relationship (when this isn't disclosed to me, it is not my fault), and finally, never sleep with someone more than three times."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421623i/837769.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She's the school slut but she's ok with that because she hates or just refuses to be in a relationship. So she made some rules and she tries to stick by them. She's lost important people in her life and she doesn't want to go through that pain again. So far it's worked out well for her.......so FAR that is....things change when you least expect them too.<br><br><i>Jaxon</i>......<br><br>He shows up in Emerson's life because they have a mutual best friend, Cole, and they end up living next door to one another. He breaks her down piece by piece....she unravels all her tight kept secrets. Because let's face it...who is not going to fall in love or lust with man a 6'plus, football player, body built for sin and tattoos. I mean right there is a recipe that's disastrous to any woman! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421625ra/837770.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"“I’ll show you how great we are going to be. Because you’re the most beautiful girl I’ve ever met, and I’m not talking about your gorgeous face, your stunning hair or your drop-dead sexy body. I never knew it was possible to be so attracted to your best friend”</b><br><br>Emerson is just so reluctant to share herself with Jaxon....I mean mentally not psychically.....she does just fine in that department. But Jaxon is just as determined to have everything from her.....he's fallen in lurve....and he can't help himself.<br><br>He sure as hell doesn't want anyone else to have her or touch her......quite the possessive little devil;)<br><br><b>“I don’t care what label you put on it, but you’re mine regardless. I won’t share.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421625ra/837771.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Im not going to tell you anymore though because you need to read the book if you want more details than that!!!!!<br><br>What worked for me in this book was, I was extremely happy not to have a sniveling virgin to read about. I seriously need a break from them!!! I also loved the secondary characters...Cole, Quinn and Jace. I was very interested in them and I can't wait for Jace's book...I think I secretly liked him better than Jaxon...sorry but true. <br><br>What didn't work for me.....I'm not sure but I never felt a strong connection to either character. However I didn't not like them at the same time, just something held me back. With that being said the book was a good quick fun read for me.....it was just ok.<br><br>I hope Jace will have a book.....I really really really liked him for some reason!!<br><br>I found this pic after I wrote this review but it actually sums up the whole book, so I thought I'd share...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421625i/837772.jpg" width="600" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Happy reading!!<br><br><i>Buddy read with one of my fav's Vishous!!!!</i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13555356797914753694" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1239894490" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1239894490" />
    <a title="Jeannine Allison" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30604562-jeannine-allison"><img alt="Jeannine Allison" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1488001283p2/30604562.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1239894490?book_show_action=true">Mar 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jeannine Allison" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jeannine Allison" href="/user/show/30604562-jeannine-allison">Jeannine Allison</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=will-read-again">will-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=tatted-heroes">tatted-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=bawling-like-a-baby">bawling-like-a-baby</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=perfect-title">perfect-title</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=favorite-couples">favorite-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=swoon">swoon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=love-the-heroine">love-the-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=sweet-guys">sweet-guys</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1239894490" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17019852782823336348"><b>*** 99c ***</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>4.5 Stars (Re-Read 7/31/2017)<br/><br/>5 Stars (First Read 11/19/2015)</i>
</b><br/><br/>I loved this!! It was definitely worth the reread. I'd forgotten how much I loved these characters. I also liked that the story took place over a large portion of the school year, giving the relationship time to grow and seem plausible. There were jumps and we didn't get to see every interaction the characters had, but that has never bothered me.<br/><br/><b>- Emerson -</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448002236ra/17080659.gif' width='500' height='275' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I've never really had an opinion on heroines (or heroes) who sleep</span>
  <span id="freeText17019852782823336348" style="display:none"><b>*** 99c ***</b><br><br><b>
  <i>4.5 Stars (Re-Read 7/31/2017)<br><br>5 Stars (First Read 11/19/2015)</i>
</b><br><br>I loved this!! It was definitely worth the reread. I'd forgotten how much I loved these characters. I also liked that the story took place over a large portion of the school year, giving the relationship time to grow and seem plausible. There were jumps and we didn't get to see every interaction the characters had, but that has never bothered me.<br><br><b>- Emerson -</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448002236ra/17080659.gif" width="500" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've never really had an opinion on heroines (or heroes) who sleep around. I know some hate 'em and some love 'em, but a character that has a lot of sex has never been a big deal for me.<br><br>What I do <i>
  <b>hate</b>
</i> is slut shaming, so I **LOVED** reading about a strong female who didn't let others shame her. I really liked the confidence and attitude that Emerson had (and held) throughout the novel. She didn't apologize for who she was, nor did she get irrationally angry when someone called her out on it. She was a very strong lead IMO, and easily one of my favorite heroines.<br><br>I also loved that she didn't go back to her old self when she so easily could have. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Jax breaks up with her (after some miscommunication and fears), and yeah she talks a good game about becoming "Em" again and hooking up with random guys, but she doesn't end up doing it. She even <i>begs</i> Jax not to leave her at the end, and I think that was awesome because she was still giving it 110% even though she was embarrassing herself. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> So many heroines (and heroes) slip back into old ways in situations like this, but she didn't. She proved she changed for good and not just for him (or because she hated being a "slut"), but for herself and I <b>loved</b> that.<br><br><b>- Jax -</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448002236ra/17080660.gif" width="500" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He was awesome, and frankly taken advantage of a little bit. I know she cared about him and she didn't actively set out to hurt him. Her goal had always been to prevent pain.<blockquote>
  <i>How come every time I wanted to avoid hurting him, all I did was hurt him more?</i>
</blockquote>So when Emerson kept saying "he's so understanding" or "of course he'll understand," I was a little annoyed. Even understanding people need to have their feelings considered, and for so long Jaxon's were kind of forgotten. But like she said, he was so understanding about it and he was so patient with her, and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I think the break up actually did a lot of good because she needed to realize that no matter her pain she had to consider him at least a <i>little</i> bit. And her initial lack of panic proved that she didn't. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I also loved how protective he was without being a douche. I know Emerson didn't really see it that way but she didn't always have the best perspective because of what she thought about her parents and relationships to realize how genuine he was. Overall, he was awesome and I didn't really dislike/not understand anything he did. Yeah, it sucked sometimes how he hurt Emerson, but like I said, he has feelings too and he also got proud and hurt just like she did so I never really thought anything he did was out of line or malicious. And I loved his really sweet moments...<blockquote>
  <i>"I realized you weren't mine at all. I. Am. Yours."</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>Cole still gave me a hard time about how I made him ask some random sorority girls to sit next to him in class that first day, so that I could get her to sit next to me.</i>
</blockquote>As far as the plot goes, it's standard NA. I don't mean that as a bad thing, it just is what it is. There is OP drama and miscommunication, which I've noticed is somewhat typical with NA reads. Sometimes it bothers me, other times it doesn't. I don't have a hard and fast rule against either of those aspects, it just depends on the story. Here I felt it worked. Did I get frustrated with their choices? Yes, absolutely. But I could also see where they were coming from. They're also young and prone to making mistakes.<br><br>The only reason for the slight deduction is that something about the last 20% left me craving a little bit more. I've become spoiled with dual POVs and I think I would have liked to have gotten more of Jax's in-depth thoughts. We do see his thoughts in the epilogue, but I wanted a better understanding of what was going on in his mind during the break-up. Like I said above, I understand why he felt he had to break up with her, but I just wish I had that insight. Particularly when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he takes Emerson out of Cole's bed... that was far too possessive for someone who broke up with her, so I would have loved his thoughts during that scene <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>Either way I loved this...<br><br>Now on to book two where I shall go fall in love with Jax's brother...<br><br>Safety: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is OP drama but there is never any technical cheating. There are definitely gray areas because their relationship is very push and pull, but I never felt like they wanted to be with other people. None of it is descriptive so it didn't bother me. *Note: I don't require my books to be safe in order to enjoy them though* <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Closure: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is an epilogue three months later where Jax and Emerson reunite after three months apart (not a separation, she was traveling). It's probably more of a HFN ending, and even though I've become a bit obsessed with detailed epilogues that take place farther in the future, I don't mind HFN in YA/NA. It feels a bit more appropriate. But Jax does have this thought in the epilogue...<blockquote><i>I already had the rock that I would slide onto her finger one day.</i></blockquote>So I was still satisfied :) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="17019852782823336348" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer581072437" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12115053112907147822"><br/><br/>I so wanted to like this book more but I just couldn't. It started really promising and I really liked Em as a character but honestly with time she became really annoying and I didn't feel anything toward her as a character except she made me feel utter frustration.<br/><br/><br/>When it comes to Em and Jax as couple.... well honestly I felt nothing there! Nothing at all! I had a feeling like author wanted to insert so much drama in first 50% that I was actually afraid to read what will happen next.<br/><br/>They as a c</span>
  <span id="freeText12115053112907147822" style="display:none"><br /><br />I so wanted to like this book more but I just couldn't. It started really promising and I really liked Em as a character but honestly with time she became really annoying and I didn't feel anything toward her as a character except she made me feel utter frustration.<br /><br /><br />When it comes to Em and Jax as couple.... well honestly I felt nothing there! Nothing at all! I had a feeling like author wanted to insert so much drama in first 50% that I was actually afraid to read what will happen next.<br /><br />They as a couple and some situations reminded me too much of BEAUTIFUL DISASTER and I just missed something all the time.<br /><br />I actually ended <b>loving side characters more then main.</b><br /><br />Cole and Quinn won my heart! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I think that their first kiss was the cutest first kiss I ever read.... so adorable!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Jace, Jax's brother.... omg I love that man and I hope there will be his book too because with every chapter I just wanted more and more of him!<br /><br />There was one situation that made me feel really bad for Em :( it was really sad to read it, finally when she decided to let go of rules/control and then..... just sad :(<br /><br />Jax was....hmmmm.... I don't know... I really didn't connect to him or to Em so much. It was like he was too much of drama. I don't know how else to describe it :( <br />He was just too much of everything in such a short time :(<br /><br />I was really wanting to give it 2 stars but then! Then Jax gave a speech which I did like even though part of it reminded me of BD again. And then came the epilogue in his POV and made it all better. <br /><br />I am a bit disappointed because I did expect something much more then I got.<br /><br />I am not sorry I read this book because I did have some fun reading it but I just missed something all the time :(<br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/618133905?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/17729712-beautiful-broken-rules">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer618133905" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14563775410368377724"><b>4 “I’m-in-love-with-Texas” Stars!!!!!!!!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421983i/839042._SY540_.jpg' alt='Slut - sketch. by calligraphuck, via Flickr' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>We all have a little slut in us, don’t we? <br/><br/>No? <br/><br/>Is it just me?</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>I’m the school slut. I hate that word; but sometimes it is what it is, or in my situation, I am what I am. I like guys, all kinds of them and lots of them.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Emerson is a slut. She knows it. She knows why she’s a slut. She has three rules that she sticks to in order to keep herself <b>safe.</b> Don’t we all create rules for ourselves to keep us safe? Even if we recognize that we’re even doing it. But</span>
  <span id="freeText14563775410368377724" style="display:none"><b>4 “I’m-in-love-with-Texas” Stars!!!!!!!!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421983i/839042._SY540_.jpg" alt="Slut - sketch. by calligraphuck, via Flickr" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>We all have a little slut in us, don’t we? <br><br>No? <br><br>Is it just me?</b><br><br><b>
  <i>I’m the school slut. I hate that word; but sometimes it is what it is, or in my situation, I am what I am. I like guys, all kinds of them and lots of them.</i>
</b><br><br>Emerson is a slut. She knows it. She knows why she’s a slut. She has three rules that she sticks to in order to keep herself <b>safe.</b> Don’t we all create rules for ourselves to keep us safe? Even if we recognize that we’re even doing it. But Emerson knows what she’s doing. She has <b>loved and lost </b>, so she needs safety to...keep her sanity……because <b>
  <i>if they aren’t cheating, they’re dying.</i>
</b><br><br><b>My Emerson:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421983i/839043._SY540_.jpg" alt="Inspiration Look - LoLoBu" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jaxon is….temptation. Even though nothing can tempt Emerson, Jaxon does. He is her kryptonite. (He’s MY kryptonite! LOL!) He is so perfect for her because <b>he pushes her</b> outside of her comfort zone and into her danger zone where she has to confront and break her rules. Jaxon breaks the walls down around Emerson’s heart, but what’s great is that she didn’t even know he was doing it. <br><br><b>
  <i>Your voice is a little like cocaine. You could bottle that stuff up and sell it. You would make a killing, especially with the sorority bimbos. Can I pay you just to talk to me all day?</i>
</b><br><br><b>My Jaxon:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421983i/839044._SY540_.jpg" alt="Men's Hair" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>”I understand what people think of me.”<br>“If they think you are beautiful, feisty, and brilliant, then I would agree with them. Anything else, I don’t care about.”<i></i></i>
</b><br><br>What’s beautiful about this book is that their love feels <b>effortless.</b> I felt myself falling with them. Yes, they had their ups and downs, but I wouldn’t call it angst. It was real stuff. They start out as friends, so their love is comfortable and I could just sink right down in it and go to sleep.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421983i/839045._SY540_.jpg" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>The contrast between his rough pulling in one hand and the sweet caress of the other was invigorating. He know I loved a little of both.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421983i/839046._SY540_.jpg" alt="Dark Chocolate Raspberry Truffles with Raspberry Dust Garnish" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Please stop running from me.”<br><br>“Please stop trying to catch me.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421983i/839047._SY540_.jpg" alt="hot air balloon" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Here’s to honor. Get on her. Stay on her. If you fall off. Get back on her. If you can’t cum in her. Cum on her!</i>
</b><br><br><i>**Note to Ms. Lauren:**<br>I love you. Too much? <br>I love how you write. It was so easy to read this story. I am fan :).</i><br><br>The next book is Jace’s story, and I am ready!!!!<br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer586144261" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer8338090354847427178"> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417019i/824262.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Oh how I loved this book!! It had been on my short list for a while but I just kept letting other things get in front of it. Wow, it was amazing!! <br/><br/>Meet Emerson<br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417019i/824263._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Your voice is a little like cocaine. You could bottle that stuff up and sell it. Can I pay you just to talk to me all day?"</i>
</b><br/><br/>She's the self proclaimed school slut. No seriously, that's the way she refers to herself. She admits openly she likes guys and sex and doesn't mind being known for it. The thing is there's things that happened </span>
  <span id="freeText8338090354847427178" style="display:none"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417019i/824262.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh how I loved this book!! It had been on my short list for a while but I just kept letting other things get in front of it. Wow, it was amazing!! <br><br>Meet Emerson<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417019i/824263._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Your voice is a little like cocaine. You could bottle that stuff up and sell it. Can I pay you just to talk to me all day?"</i>
</b><br><br>She's the self proclaimed school slut. No seriously, that's the way she refers to herself. She admits openly she likes guys and sex and doesn't mind being known for it. The thing is there's things that happened in her past that makes her avoid relationships at all costs. So she made up a set of rules to protect herself. <br><b><br>1)Never sleep with someone that a friend has feelings for.<br>2)Never sleep with someone who is in a known relationship.<br>3)Never sleep with someone more than three times. <br></b><br>Everything was working out fine in her life with these rules until the morning she met Jaxon Riley.<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417019i/824264.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"You have to stop worrying that you'll lose me. There's nowhere else in this world that I want to be. I love you, beautiful girl."</i>
</b><br><br>At first glance she notices how gorgeous he is. But then when she finds out he's the guy that is going to be moving in next door with her best friend. They start out as quick friends but over time start growing closer and closer. She knows she wants him and that it will eventually happen between them, but once it does she realizes that he's different and trouble for her with a capital T. Soon enough Jaxon starts breaking down her walls but with the fears she's had her whole life about being left and cheated on nothing comes easy for for them. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417019ra/824265.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Please stop running from me,"he whispered.<br>"Please stop trying to catch me,"she said getting up to leave.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417019i/824266.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story was amazing. I absolutely adored Jaxon. He was was hot all around. I have a thing for tattoos, bad boys on bikes, and football players. He was all of the above. Not to mention he was so sweet, and had the most unbelievable amount of patience. I loved the fact that even when Em was being "hard to get along with" <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(taking all of those guys upstairs) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and trying to push Jaxon away he was there to make sure she was alright even when it was killing him.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br> And Emerson, yeah, she's not your typical heroine, but come on she was quirky and spoke her mind. She wasn't ashamed of who she was either. I didn't 100% agree with everything she did, especially when it came to decisions related to Jax but she learned from her mistakes and owned them. And she never tried to be something that she wasn't.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Tell me that you want me,"he whispered.<br>"I want you." Always.<br>"Only me?"<br>"Only you." Had there ever been anyone else?</i>
</b> <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417019ra/824268.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story also had amazing secondary characters. Quinn, Cole, and Jace. I loved these characters just as much as the primary characters, and I would give anything to be in their little click to hang out and watch movies or catch a frat party. Cole and Quinn are like the worlds best friends EVER!!! And then Jace, OMG he needs his own book. I want to know so much more about him. Hell, I want to know more about all of these characters. As much as I want Jace to have a book I feel like I need a little bit more from Jax and Emerson. What happens next, can everything just automatically be a HEA between them? I mean the guy in the end was preparing..."for a future" with her and I want know I need to read about it. Read this book, whatever you do it's amazing and will not leave you disappointed. :)<br><br><i>"I just met you and I'm amazed by you already.<br>You beauty has me blind to all others.<br>One day you'll let someone in and he'll be a lucky bastard.<br>One day you are going to discover how beautiful and strong you are.<br>I hope that I'm standing right next to you holding your hand when you do.</i><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417020i/824269.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15324948159678770015">After noticing how many books I have in my paused folder on my Kindle, I decided that I would for the foreseeable future try - however hard it may be, to finish them.<br/><br/>I hate pausing books. It's a complete waste of money, though at the same time it's hardly putting a hole in my wallet with the little they do cost on Kindle. At least that's what I tell myself at the time.<br/><br/>I'll most likely regret putting myself through the torture of re-reading paused books, especially the ones where I cant remember </span>
  <span id="freeText15324948159678770015" style="display:none">After noticing how many books I have in my paused folder on my Kindle, I decided that I would for the foreseeable future try - however hard it may be, to finish them.<br><br>I hate pausing books. It's a complete waste of money, though at the same time it's hardly putting a hole in my wallet with the little they do cost on Kindle. At least that's what I tell myself at the time.<br><br>I'll most likely regret putting myself through the torture of re-reading paused books, especially the ones where I cant remember why I did it in the first place.<br><br>There are only two reasons I, and I'm guessing everyone else pauses books - and that's:<br><b>1. They suck! You cant go on, or you may just break out in hives.<br>Or.<br>2. A book that cant possibly wait to be read, has just caught your eye.</b><br><br>At the time i re-picked this book up, I couldn't recall which category to place this.<br>Now that I've read it, it's definitely the former.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386295717ra/7331919.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_ml01gvUPCG1r18fjgo1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now don't get me wrong, I did actually to an extent enjoy the first few chapters. Emerson wasn't TOO bad a character at the time, to read. Also the Riley brothers were HOT to trot.<br>However after a while I started to despise Emerson.<br>Actually as soon as that happened, I completely recalled why this book was shelved in the first place. Emerson.<br>I hated her reasoning behind why she was, in short - A whore.<br>Someone not wanting to be tied down by anyone.<br>Sure it was a horrible experience, but her 'life lessons' that were taken from that horrible experience and her conclusions were totally unreasonable. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ How can you come to the conclusion that your parents are cheating with each other just by them being in the same car together? They were her parents?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>And then base your whole life around your assumption of what you thought happened. The whole thing just seemed ridiculous.<br><br>The feelings between her and Jaxon didn't translate to me. I at times found myself skipping over words without reading them, bored out of my brains - to be completely honest.<br><br>If I had to pick a character from the bunch that I didn't want to destroy, it'd have to be Jace!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_613661572" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/613661572" />
    <a title="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9816167-jessica-s-book-review"><img alt="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454474452p2/9816167.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/613661572?book_show_action=true">May 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/9816167-jessica-s-book-review">Jessica&#39;s Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/17729712-beautiful-broken-rules">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer613661572" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8898972893311457339"><b> <a href='http://jessicasbookreview.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Read More Reviews </a> | <a href='https://www.facebook.com/JessicasBookReview' rel='nofollow noopener'>Find Me on Facebook</a> </b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“One thing I know for sure and have come to terms with- I’m the school slut.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421323i/836802._SY540_.jpg' width='325' height='448' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Yep, that is Emerson or Em as she likes to be called. That is how you are introduced to Em on the very first page and well, she is right; she’s the school slut. Em has had a lot of loss & pain in her life. Her parents died when she was 15 and she learned love does not last forever. Either they die or they cheat on you. Because of this she has created three rules to live by w</span>
  <span id="freeText8898972893311457339" style="display:none"><b> <a href="http://jessicasbookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Read More Reviews </a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/JessicasBookReview" rel="nofollow noopener">Find Me on Facebook</a> </b><br><br><b>
  <i>“One thing I know for sure and have come to terms with- I’m the school slut.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421323i/836802._SY540_.jpg" width="325" height="448" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yep, that is Emerson or Em as she likes to be called. That is how you are introduced to Em on the very first page and well, she is right; she’s the school slut. Em has had a lot of loss &amp; pain in her life. Her parents died when she was 15 and she learned love does not last forever. Either they die or they cheat on you. Because of this she has created three rules to live by when it comes to men.<br><br><b>Em’s Rules:<br>1)	Never sleep with someone a friend has feelings for.<br>2)	Never sleep with someone else’s boyfriend/husband.<br>3)	Never sleep with someone more than three times. </b><br><br>Em lives by these rules; she makes no exceptions for anyone. She thinks she is happy with this arrangement and all she needs is her two best friends, Cole &amp; Quinn. Everything changes when Em meets Jaxon and suddenly everything changes no matter who hard Em tries to make Jax the same as all the other boys before him.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421323i/836803.jpg" width="325" height="406" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421323i/836804.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421323i/836805.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I will be honest, at first I hated Emerson. Forget the fact she is HOT with an amazing body and D cup boobs, she is a slut. She sleeps around and doesn’t care. It took me awhile to get into her character. you do not often read a story where the girl is the “bad” girl who doesn’t “do relationships.” I loved the story and the other characters especially Cole but Em took some getting used to. Then it changed and I begin to understand Em and what she has been through to make her feel &amp; act the way she does with men. I begin to really love her character. She is way more than the <i>“school slut”</i> as she puts it.<br><br>Jax is amazing. I want a Jax is my life to love and adore me no matter my past or how hard I want him out. I want a man that would fight for me like Jax does for Em and I fell completely in love with him myself. Jax moves to Southern California from Texas for college and the fact he is a football star makes him even HOTTER. He has his own past but not like Em; he’ll do anything to be with her and force her to open up to him. Did I mention he has a twin, an identical twin… oh my…<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421323i/836806.jpg" width="325" height="306" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>Your beauty has me blind to all others.<br>My eyes will always find you in a crowd.<br>My favorite part of the day is when I get to hear you laugh.<br>One day you’ll let someone in and he’ll be a lucky bastard.<br>One day you are going to discover how beautiful and strong you are.<br>I hope that I’m standing right next to you holding your hand when you do.</i>
</b><br><br>Beautiful Broken Rules is not only a wonderful romance novel with hot men, yep plural! It has depth and emotional, more than I ever thought. I love when a fun book becomes so much more and Beautiful Broken Rules is just that. I read the book within a day, not because it is short but because I could not put it down! I just had to read the scene when Em’s emotional wall would come falling down and finally let Jax in her heart. I knew the scene would be epic and it was.<br><br>Ms. Kimberly Lauren did a fantastic job with the characters. I felt so emotionally invested in all 5 characters from Emerson &amp; Jax, to Quinn &amp; Cole, and even Jace (Jaxon’s twin). I loved each and every character and would love to read a book about any one of them, especially Jace **<i>
  <b>hint, hint</b>
</i>**. <br><br>This is just a fantastic story that is unique and different in every way. I am so honored the author gave me an ARC copy to read &amp; review because I adored this story. Thank you Kimberly Lauren!<br><br>I hope everyone reads Beautiful Broken Rules and falls in love with the characters and storyline just like I did. You won’t be disappointed!<br><br>I give Beautiful Broken Rules 4.5 Stars.<br><br><br><i>ARC provided by the author in return for an honest review.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="8898972893311457339" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10234100782197443748"><b>3.5~Stars</b><br/><br/>I started out <i>totally</i> loving this book. Praise sweet virgin baby Buddha, finally a girl that gets to wear the dick for once. I'm so sick of hot manwhores with their de-virginizing overalls popping cherries right and left.<br/><br/>In <i>Beautifully Broken Rules</i> the girl gets to do the sleeping around. The girl gets to be the dude! And it. Is. Awesome!!!! It was about damn time a confident, sexual heroine took her "I love sex" axe and chopped down the damn cherry tree! Hooray!!!!!!<br/><br/>However, once I got</span>
  <span id="freeText10234100782197443748" style="display:none"><b>3.5~Stars</b><br /><br />I started out <i>totally</i> loving this book. Praise sweet virgin baby Buddha, finally a girl that gets to wear the dick for once. I'm so sick of hot manwhores with their de-virginizing overalls popping cherries right and left.<br /><br />In <i>Beautifully Broken Rules</i> the girl gets to do the sleeping around. The girl gets to be the dude! And it. Is. Awesome!!!! It was about damn time a confident, sexual heroine took her "I love sex" axe and chopped down the damn cherry tree! Hooray!!!!!!<br /><br />However, once I got over my female heroine crush, I was left with a really good story, but not necessarily an OH MY GOD great story. After a while, I started to get a little bored. With such a strong start, I guess I expected it to keep up that momentum. Too much started to be told to me and I wanted...I wanted a little bit...<i>more</i>.<br /><br />I am extremely glad I read this book. You will completely fall in love with the characters, firstdary <i>and</i> secondary. What it lacks in plot; it definitely rebounds with some pretty bad ass characters!<br /><br />READ ON!<br /><br />More reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blogspot.com">http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blo...</a></span>

        rated it

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6538604-nikki?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6538604-nikki?shelf=sweet-romance">sweet-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6538604-nikki?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer618917527" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16229885630686694553"><b>5 Incredible Amazing Can't believe this is a debut novel I have a new favorite author stars! :-) </b><br/><br/>So I'm just going along doing my GR thing... And I get a book rec from a friend for this book. Like I usually do, I check out the blurb and see what its all about then check the recommender's review. After all that I check the price. <br/><br/>* Blurb sounded pretty awesome: ✔<br/>* Review is enough to make me want to read it: ✔<br/>* Price is one that I'm willing to pay: ✔ <br/><br/>So I one click and decide to go ahead and star</span>
  <span id="freeText16229885630686694553" style="display:none"><b>5 Incredible Amazing Can't believe this is a debut novel I have a new favorite author stars! :-) </b><br><br>So I'm just going along doing my GR thing... And I get a book rec from a friend for this book. Like I usually do, I check out the blurb and see what its all about then check the recommender's review. After all that I check the price. <br><br>* Blurb sounded pretty awesome: ✔<br>* Review is enough to make me want to read it: ✔<br>* Price is one that I'm willing to pay: ✔ <br><br>So I one click and decide to go ahead and start right then since I wasn't reading anything else at that moment. <br><br><b>I. Did. Not. Want. To. Put. It. Down!</b><br><br>Curse my work schedule! As soon as I finished the first couple pages I knew I should have waited till the next day to start this, seeing as I had to go to bed to get up at O'dark early! :| Then I had to suffer through my few hours at work till I could get home and get back to the <b>AWESOMENESS</b> that is this book! I freaking loved it! The first meeting between Jaxon and Emerson was to die for hilarious! That girl had balls! I loved her! Jaxon (and Jace by default, seeing as they had the same face <span>[image error]</span>) were so swoon worthy.<br> I have found my next book boyfriend(s)! <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/64824.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The story here is one that is at times heartbreaking and at others so sweet and melt your heart gooey that I just wanted to jump in there and live it with these amazing characters. The way Emerson had closed herself off was so sad but then Jax came along and he plowed right through her barriers. Girl never stood a chance! All the characters here were so well written that I really felt a connection to them all. I was invested in them and determined to see them to their HEA's. Even down to Jaxon's mom who we only met once and same with Ellie. They were such minor characters that somehow played major roles. Jace, Cole and Quinn were the best friends a girl in Emerson's situation (or anyone really) could have asked for. I want to say so much more but I fear I'll spoil things and for once, I don't want to give any spoilers! This was a really great book! I was really surprised to learn it was a debut too. The author's style was a perfect fit for me and I can't wait to read more from her! And for those that are curious, I asked to make sure and <u>there WILL be a book for Jace.</u> (Although the date is unknown)</span>

<div id="review_2101423971" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2101423971" />
    <a title="Whitney" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66575688-whitney"><img alt="Whitney" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593665089p2/66575688.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2101423971?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Whitney" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Whitney" href="/user/show/66575688-whitney">Whitney</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66575688-whitney?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66575688-whitney?shelf=audio-book">audio-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66575688-whitney?shelf=4-star-reads">4-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66575688-whitney?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66575688-whitney?shelf=kindle-unlimited">kindle-unlimited</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2101423971" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8513690600448950998">I have a lot of mixed feelings about this book. Let's talk about the good, the bad, and the ugly... Shall we?<br/><br/><b>
  <u>The Good:</u>
</b><br/><br/>Anything written during <i>the college years</i> instantly bring me back in time. It is so nostalgic for me. Lauren's writing helped me relive those cherished times. Her storytelling was spot on. I was hopelessly caught up in this story. Through all the drama and conflict, I couldn't quit it. I <s>wanted</s> needed to know what was going to happen. Her characters were so developed and pers</span>
  <span id="freeText8513690600448950998" style="display:none">I have a lot of mixed feelings about this book. Let's talk about the good, the bad, and the ugly... Shall we?<br><br><b>
  <u>The Good:</u>
</b><br><br>Anything written during <i>the college years</i> instantly bring me back in time. It is so nostalgic for me. Lauren's writing helped me relive those cherished times. Her storytelling was spot on. I was hopelessly caught up in this story. Through all the drama and conflict, I couldn't quit it. I <s>wanted</s> needed to know what was going to happen. Her characters were so developed and personable. The friendships were envious.<br><br><b>
  <u>The Bad:</u>
</b><br><br>Speaking of friendships, why the hell do they put up with Emerson's crap!? I get that she is a deeply flawed character, but she is selfish and a tad bit bitchy. One could argue that Quinn held the crew together; she is Em's sister, and Cole probably puts up with Em for Quinn. But, how does one explain Jace? He literally takes Emerson's side over his brother. WTF?<br><br>Poor Jax always got the short end of the stick. Emerson decides to flee to do something ridiculous or melodramatic, but her too-perfect boytoy gets the blame. EVERY. TIME. Jax is upset that she keeps running off to do stupid shit but that somehow makes him the bad guy. And heaven-forbid that he should stand up for himself and express his feelings. He hurt Em by telling her HOW HE FELT, so now he's a douche. <b>*rolls eyes*</b><br><br>I hated that aspect of the book. <br><br>Now for the <b>
  <u>The Ugly:</u>
</b><br><br>I'm a busy gal. Most people like to listen to music while running errands, doing housework, or working out - not me. I prefer to listen to audiobooks. Yep, I opted for the audiobook. <i>What a mistake...</i> While she did a fantastic job of storytelling and expressing emotion, her voice acting was terrible. Emerson's voice was over-the-top Californian Valley girl. Quinn's voice was pitchy and childish. But the worst of all? <b>Jax.</b> He sounded like an old Cajun lady who was recovering from laryngitis. <b>I cannot get all swoony over an old lady with laryngitis!</b> And Emerson already irked me, but when you added in her annoying voice....<br><br><b>#purerage</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503755717ra/23691787.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can't really explain it, but I still want to give this book <b>4 stars.</b> I feel like if I would have actually read the book over listening to it, I would have enjoyed it more. I am still certain that Emerson would have still annoyed me, but without that terrible voice, she would have been more tolerable. I also could have really enjoyed Jax's character more. He would have been attractive and swoon-worthy. The story is really good. And I love it takes place over an extended period of time. Lauren let the reader really get to see the characters grow and mature. <br><br>So, <b>4 stars?</b> *shrugs*</span>
  <a data-text-id="8513690600448950998" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6rhYBltjk7fBh5EUKcb/zQoQVCsajg/Me+SDh1dYcv0/cNmIntu9kTFHtkXxpVpf6CFtwEyNU/0izqp4ctKYTA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('N2usUrbkWL7Uqt5U1MN9pvn0NbACqCRLBrL1b5Nzv8Pioy3cc1x2mCRq+QUMoNg0G8UMW1SreHpfmNyQtvlVcg==')})
  }
